### [1] [Large Language Models as Unified Multimodal Learners for Clinical Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15380)
*Ajay Madhavan Ravichandran,Bilgin Osmandoja,Klemens Budde,Klaus Netter,Tobias Strapatsas,Aljoscha Burchardt,Sebastian Möller,Roland Roller*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出将电子健康记录中所有模态的数据（文本、生命体征、实验室值等）统一转化为单一自然语言序列，直接微调预训练语言模型，无需任何特定任务的多模态融合架构。在住院死亡率、移植失败预测和急诊分诊三个任务上，该方法达到或超过专门设计的多模态基线，并优于临床部署的梯度提升模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有临床预测系统依赖任务特定的多模态融合架构，需要为每个新任务和临床场景重新设计编码器和组合机制，系统复杂度高且缺乏通用性。

Method: 将所有患者数据（不论模态）转化为单一自然语言序列，直接端到端微调预训练语言模型（包括ModernBERT、Llama 3.1、Gemma、DeepSeek-R1-Qwen、Qwen3），无需任何架构修改用于融合。

Result: 在MIMIC-III住院死亡率、德国移植中心的移植物失败预测、救护车记录急诊分诊三个任务上，统一文本序列化方法匹配或超过传统多模态基线，并在移植物失败预测任务中优于临床部署的梯度提升模型。

Conclusion: 单一序列化范式足以应对多模态临床预测，无需定制融合架构，大幅降低系统复杂度的同时性能不输甚至超过专门设计的方法。

Abstract: Electronic health records combine free-text clinical narratives with structured measurements such as vital signs, laboratory values, and comorbidities. Yet most clinical prediction systems still rely on task-specific fusion architectures, pairing dedicated encoders for each modality with learned combination mechanisms that must be re-engineered for every new task and clinical setting. We propose a simpler alternative: convert all patient data, regardless of modality, into a single natural language sequence and fine-tune a pretrained language model end-to-end, with no architectural modification for fusion. We evaluate this approach across three clinically distinct prediction tasks: in-hospital mortality on MIMIC-III, graft failure prediction using longitudinal data from a German transplant center, and emergency triage classification from ambulance records - comparing encoder-based (ModernBERT) and decoder-based (Llama 3.1, Gemma, DeepSeek-R1-Qwen, Qwen3) fine-tuning against established multimodal baselines and, for graft failure, a gradient boosting model currently used in clinical practice for post-transplant patient management. Across all three tasks, unified textual serialization matches or exceeds task-specific multimodal baselines, and outperforms the clinically deployed gradient boosting system on graft failure prediction. These results indicate that a single serialization-based paradigm, without bespoke fusion architectures, is sufficient for multimodal clinical prediction - substantially reducing system complexity while matching or exceeding specialized designs.

</details>


### [2] [Verbalizable Representations Form a Global Workspace in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15495)
*Wes Gurnee,Nicholas Sofroniew,Adam Pearce,Mateusz Piotrowski,Isaac Kauvar,Runjin Chen,Anna Soligo,Paul Bogdan,Euan Ong,Rowan Wang,Ben Thompson,David Abrahams,Subhash Kantamneni,Emmanuel Ameisen,Joshua Batson,Jack Lindsey*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大型语言模型中存在一个与人类意识访问功能类似的"J空间"（Jacobian镜头识别出的表征集合），它具备全局工作区的特性：内容可报告、可主动调取、可用于静默推理，且承载约数十个概念。该空间揭示了模型在未输出前的战略思考、评估意识和训练内化的错误倾向，同时提出了一种通过干预工作区内容来改善模型行为的"反事实反思训练"方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类大脑处理的信息中仅少数能被意识访问（即可言语报告、受控推理等），作者希望探究大型语言模型中是否也存在类似的功能性区分，并开发工具来识别和理解这种"可意识访问"的表征。

Method: 提出了一种新的可解释性技术——Jacobian lens，用以识别模型在处理过程中准备"言语化"的表征（J-space）。通过分析这些表征的功能属性（可报告性、可主动调用、可用于静默推理等）和结构特征（中层出现、承载数十概念、广泛广播），与全局工作区理论进行对比验证。

Result: J-space具备全局工作区的功能特征：内容可被报告、主动召唤和维持、用于承载静默推理的中间步骤，可作为任意下游计算的参数传递；同时具有意识访问的结构特征：仅在中层携带连贯内容、同时承载约数十个概念、被模型权重广播更广泛。在对齐审计中，J-space揭示了模型的战略思考、评估意识和训练内化的错误倾向。

Conclusion: 语言模型中存在一个小型、特权的表征集合，承载着人类意识访问的部分功能特征。解码这些表征有助于理解模型正在进行的认知过程。后训练将"助手"的观点安装到工作区中；提出的反事实反思训练通过只训练模型在被中断并要求反思时会说什么来改善行为。

Abstract: Out of everything the human brain processes, only a small fraction is consciously accessible, in the sense of being available for verbal report, deliberate control, and flexible reasoning. In this paper, we present evidence that an analogous functional distinction has emerged in large language models. Using a new interpretability technique, the Jacobian lens, we identify the representations a model is poised to verbalize at any point in its processing. These representations, which we collectively call the J-space, exhibit the functional properties characteristic of a global workspace: their contents can be reported, deliberately summoned and held, used to carry the intermediate steps of silent reasoning, and passed as arguments to arbitrary downstream computations, while automatic processing such as text parsing and routine inference proceeds without them. The J-space also has structural signatures that global workspace theory associates with conscious access: it carries coherent content only in an intermediate band of layers, holds on the order of tens of concepts at a time, and is broadcast by the model's weights more widely than other representations. These properties make it a practical window into a model's unspoken thinking. In alignment audits, it reveals strategic deliberation, evaluation awareness, and trained-in misaligned dispositions that never appear in the model's outputs. We find that post-training installs the Assistant's point of view in the workspace, and we introduce counterfactual reflection training, which improves behavior by training only what a model would say if interrupted and asked to reflect. These results indicate that language models maintain a small, privileged set of representations bearing some of the functional hallmarks of conscious access, and that decoding these representations sheds light on ongoing cognitive processes.

</details>


### [3] [VarRate: Training-Free Variable-Rate KV Cache Compression for Long-Context LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15498)
*Shahrzad Esmat,Dhawal Shah,Ali Jannesari*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: VarRate提出了一种免训练的可变低秩KV缓存压缩方法，通过为每个token分配与查询显著性相关的可变秩预算，保留所有token而非丢弃，在20%预算下LongBench任务中仅下降0.8个点，显著优于不可逆的token选择方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有两类免训练的KV缓存压缩方法存在结构性缺陷：token选择方法（如SnapKV、Ada-KV）重要性信号退化时准确率骤降11-15点；均匀低秩编码虽保留所有token但浪费预算。两者都缺乏按需分配秩预算的能力。

Method: VarRate是一种免训练的KV编解码器，根据每个token的查询显著性（query salience）为其分配可变的低秩预算，确保每个token保持非零秩，实现秩分配而非token驱逐。

Result: 在LongBench（16个任务）上，20%预算下VarRate在Llama-3.1-8B和Qwen2.5-7B上仅比未压缩模型下降0.8个点。相比查询感知选择方法仅下降3.5-5.5点，显著优于均匀秩消融实验，与KVzip精度相当但预填充开销仅为其1/8。

Conclusion: VarRate通过免训练的变秩分配策略，在保留所有token的前提下实现了高压缩率与高精度的平衡，避免了不可逆驱逐带来的精度崩塌，是当前最强的匹配内存压缩器。

Abstract: The key-value (KV) cache is the main memory bottleneck in long-context large language model (LLM) inference. Two leading training-free families are both structurally limited: token-selection methods (SnapKV, Ada-KV) score importance from an observation window and evict low-scoring tokens, but eviction is irreversible -- so when the importance signal degrades under query-agnostic reuse, accuracy collapses by 11-15 points; uniform low-rank coding keeps every token but spends equal rank everywhere, wasting budget. We observe that both failures share one cure: rank should be allocated, not evicted. We present VarRate, a training-free KV codec that assigns each token a variable low-rank budget by its query salience, keeping every token at a nonzero rank. Comparable adaptive-rank codecs reach this allocation only through training; VarRate requires none. Because no token is dropped, it degrades by only 3.5-5.5 points where query-aware selection collapses. At a matched 20% budget on LongBench (16 tasks), VarRate stays within 0.8 points of the uncompressed model on both Llama-3.1-8B and Qwen2.5-7B. Averaged over the two, it is the strongest matched-memory compressor. It significantly beats its uniform-rank ablation on both models. Against KVzip, a method purpose-built for query-agnostic reuse, it is accuracy-equivalent in three of four settings and within a point overall, at about one-eighth the prefill overhead.

</details>


### [4] [EpiNarrate: Agentic Generation of Grounded Narratives from Epidemiological Scenario Projections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15544)
*Rituparna Datta,Srini Venkatramanan,Bryan L. Lewis,Yiqi Su,Harry Hochheiser,Lucie Contamin,Parantapa Bhattacharya,Naren Ramakrishnan,Anil Vullikanti*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为EpiNarrate的智能体框架，用于自动生成公共卫生报告。该框架将结构化数值推理与自然语言生成相分离，通过提取场景轴、构建偏序模式、构建增广数据集、引入基于最大熵原理的有趣性驱动选择机制等步骤，有效解决了直接使用大型语言模型（LLM）对大规模流行病学集成数据进行摘要和情境化时产生的不一致、遗漏和脆弱性问题。在COVID-19情景建模中心的实验表明，该方法能够生成事实基础更强、流行病学模式覆盖更广且风格贴近专家撰写的报告。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 公共卫生报告需要将复杂的流行病学预测以清晰、可理解的方式传达给政策制定者和公众，但直接使用大规模语言模型（LLM）对多维集成数据进行总结和情境化时，容易出现不一致、信息遗漏和结果不稳健的问题。

Method: 提出EpiNarrate框架，分离结构化数值推理与自然语言生成。具体包括：1) 提取场景轴并构建偏序模式，实现多维空间的系统遍历；2) 构建增广数据集，通过比较语法推导语义和算术一致的量化陈述；3) 基于最大熵原理引入有趣性驱动的选择机制，平衡覆盖度与不冗余性。

Result: 在COVID-19情景建模中心数据集上的实验表明，EpiNarrate生成的报告比直接使用LLM具有更强的事实基础、更广泛的流行病学模式覆盖，同时能够保持专家撰写报告的风格。

Conclusion: 通过将结构化推理与语言生成解耦，并结合有趣性驱动的选择机制，可以有效提升大模型在多维数据情境化报告生成中的事实准确性和覆盖度，为公共卫生叙事生成提供了新的方法论框架。

Abstract: Generation of clear and accessible public health narratives is critical for communicating complex epidemiological projections to policymakers and the general public at large. Such narratives require more than simply reporting numbers: projections must be contextualized and quantitatively grounded across multiple dimensions. Further, projections are often derived from large ensemble datasets which combine intervention assumptions, geographic and demographic strata, outcomes, time horizons, and uncertainty quantiles. However, directly using large language models (LLMs) to summarize and contextualize such data often leads to inconsistencies, omissions, and fragile behavior. We introduce an agentic framework (EpiNarrate) for public health report generation that separates structured numerical reasoning from natural-language generation. The framework first extracts scenario axes and organizes them into a partial-order schema, enabling systematic traversal of the underlying multidimensional space. It then constructs an augmented dataset and derives valid quantitative statements through a comparison grammar that enforces semantic and arithmetic consistency. To balance coverage and non-redundancy, we introduce an interestingness-driven selection mechanism based on maximum-entropy principles. Experiments on the COVID-19 Scenario Modeling Hub demonstrate that our model produces narratives with improved factual grounding and broader coverage of salient epidemiological patterns, while preserving the style of expert-written reports.

</details>


### [5] [SkillCorpus: Consolidating and Evaluating the Open Skill Ecosystem for Real-World LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15557)
*Yanze Wang,Pengfei Yao,Tianyi Sun,Chuanrui Hu,Yan Xiao,Yunyun Han,Jun Sun,Yafeng Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SkillCorpus框架，从约82.1万爬取的技能中通过多阶段流水线筛选出96,401个高质量技能，构建了包含16类分类法和三维质量评估（实用性、鲁棒性、安全性）的技能语料库，并配备检索-选择模型。在三个基准上集成SkillCorpus均带来一致性提升，最大提升7.5个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前开源社区存在大量碎片化、冗余、质量参差不齐的Agent技能文件（SKILL.md），缺乏统一整理和评估体系，无法有效支撑实际智能体任务。核心问题是如何整合这些分散的技能资源并量化其真实价值。

Method: 构建SkillCorpus框架，包含多阶段流水线：爬取约82.1万技能→筛选过滤→按16类分类法组织→从实用性、鲁棒性、安全性三个质量维度评估→微调检索-选择模型以匹配任务相关技能。在三个基准上使用两种框架和两种开源基座模型进行端到端评估。

Result: SkillCorpus在SkillsBench（+7.5pp）、GDPVal、QwenClawBench三个基准上均带来一致性能提升。操作分析表明收益来源于覆盖边界和框架边界两个因素。

Conclusion: SkillCorpus是首个端到端证明经过整理和检索服务的社区技能语料库能提升真实Agent任务性能的研究，同时明确了其适用边界和局限性。

Abstract: Agent skills, SKILL.md files that package reusable procedural knowledge for an LLM agent, are a popular mechanism for extending agent capabilities. Public repositories now host them in large and growing numbers, yet these artifacts are fragmented, redundant, and uneven in quality, and their value in practice is unclear. A core question remains open, namely how to consolidate this open-source SKILL.md ecosystem into a single usable corpus, and what bounds its benefit on real-world agent tasks. We present SkillCorpus, a framework that aggregates, curates, matches, and evaluates the open skill ecosystem at scale. It filters ~821,000 crawled skills through a multi-stage pipeline into 96,401 skills organised by a 16-class taxonomy and three quality facets (utility, robustness, safety), and pairs them with a fine-tuned retrieval-and-selection stack that matches task-relevant skills. We evaluate end-to-end across three benchmarks (SkillsBench, GDPVal, QwenClawBench), two harnesses, and two open backbones with a frontier robustness check. Integrating SkillCorpus yields consistent gains across all three benchmarks, largest on SkillsBench (+7.5 pp). An operational analysis traces the gains to a coverage boundary and a harness boundary. SkillCorpus is, to our knowledge, the first end-to-end account of when a curated, retrieval-served community corpus improves real agent tasks, and where it does not. The dataset, models, and code will be released upon acceptance.

</details>


### [6] [Process Reward Informed Tree Rollout for Effective Multi-Turn RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15610)
*Xintong Li,Sha Li,Yuwei Zhang,Changlong Yu,Rongmei Lin,Hongye Jin,Shuyi Guan,Xin Liu,Linwei Li,Qingyu Yin,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出PATR框架，利用过程反馈指导树状轨迹展开，在长周期智能体强化学习中优先从有前景的状态分支、复用共享前缀并终止无效路径，从而在相同训练预算下提升探索效率，在SWE-Bench和FrozenLake上分别提升最高5.0和9.3个点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRPO/RLOO等RL方法在长周期智能体任务中采用均匀回滚策略，浪费预算在无信息的死胡同尝试上，而中间有前景状态探索不足。需要一种更高效的探索策略来优化有限训练预算的利用。

Method: PATR框架：1) 利用任务相关的过程反馈对部分轨迹评分；2) 从高评分状态选择性分支；3) 复用共享前缀避免重复采样；4) 保守终止退化路径减少浪费。生成的轨迹组兼容标准策略优化方法。

Result: 在SWE-Bench上提升最高+5.0分，在FrozenLake上提升最高+9.3分，验证了过程引导的树状回滚策略在多轮RL中的有效性。

Conclusion: 过程引导的树状展开是一种高效且可扩展的多轮强化学习策略，能够显著提升长周期智能体任务的训练效果。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a key approach for training LLM agents, yet popular methods such as GRPO/RLOO rely on multiple independently sampled complete trajectories for advantage estimation. In long-horizon agentic tasks, such a uniform rollout strategy can waste budget on uninformative dead-end attempts, while promising intermediate states do not receive sufficient exploration. The multi-turn structure of agentic trajectories, with interleaved actions and observations, naturally supports organizing a trajectory group as a tree, where each turn serves as a decision point for exploration. This perspective reframes effective exploration as the problem of deciding where to branch. We propose Process-Scorer Guided Adaptive Tree Rollout (PATR), a quality-aware rollout framework for multi-turn agent RL. PATR uses task-appropriate process feedback to score partial trajectories, selectively branches from promising states, reuses shared prefixes, and conservatively stops degenerate paths to reduce wasted sampling. The resulting rollout groups remain compatible with standard policy optimization while providing more efficient exploration under the same training budget. We evaluate PATR on FrozenLake and the challenging SWE-Bench, which is largely unexplored by prior tree-rollout agent RL methods. Experiments show that PATR improves performance by up to +5.0 points on SWE-Bench and +9.3 points on FrozenLake, highlighting process-guided tree rollouts as an effective strategy for scalable multi-turn RL.

</details>


### [7] [On the Structure of Address in Multi-Party Dialogue: From Discrete Labels to Continuous Levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15648)
*Taiga Mori,Koji Inoue,Divesh Lala,Tatsuya Kawahara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究多轮多人对话中的"接收者检测"问题，提出将地址（address）视为连续现象而非离散类别。通过分析多人对话语料库中的标注数据，作者构建了二元标签和连续地址水平，并发现连续模型比离散模型能更好地预测对话行为（如视线、反馈信号），表明地址具有分级结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法将对话中的"接收者检测"视为多分类离散任务，仅用于预测话轮转换。作者认为这种假设可能过于简化，需要重新审视地址（address）是否本质上是连续现象。

Method: 1) 使用多人对话语料库进行多标注者标注；2) 构建基于多数投票的二元地址标签；3) 利用潜变量模型从标注者判断中推断连续地址水平；4) 比较两种表示与话轮转换、视线、反馈信号的关系。

Result: 1) 除了话轮转换，视线和反馈信号也与地址相关联；2) 使用连续地址水平的模型比使用离散标签的模型具有更好的预测拟合度。

Conclusion: 地址可能具有分级结构（graded structure），未来接收者检测研究应考虑地址的连续性质，而非仅视为离散分类问题。

Abstract: In multi-party dialogues between a dialogue system and multiple users, identifying to whom an utterance is addressed is a key challenge. Prior work has typically treated addressee detection as a multi-class classification task, selecting a single label representing an individual participant or the group. This formulation assumes that address is inherently discrete and has primarily been used for predicting turn-taking. In this paper, we revisit this assumption by analyzing address as a continuous phenomenon. Using a multi-party human dialogue corpus annotated by multiple annotators, we construct both binary address labels derived from majority-vote addressee labels and continuous address levels inferred from annotator judgments using a latent-variable model. We then examine how these representations relate to turn-taking as well as listener behaviors, including gaze and backchannels. Our results show that, in addition to turn-taking, both gaze and backchannels are associated with address. Furthermore, models using continuous address levels achieve better predictive fit than those using discrete labels, suggesting that address may exhibit graded structure. Finally, we discuss the future directions of addressee detection research based on the findings of this study.

</details>


### [8] [Adaptive Multi-Step Lookahead Decoding for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15655)
*Yingqian Cui,Wei Deng,Lantao Mei,Hang Li,Charu C. Aggarwal,Hui Liu,Yue Xing*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出AdaLook，一种自适应前瞻框架，用于掩码扩散语言模型的并行文本生成解码。它根据候选分数方差动态决定是否继续展开，并在中间状态需要额外探索时进行分支扩展，在多个基准上取得了优于现有一步前瞻方法的准确率-解码步数权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前瞻解码方法主要依赖浅层的一步前瞻，只能优化即时信息增益，对于长程解码轨迹效果不佳；而简单的深层前瞻扩展又因固定深度展开导致计算冗余，无法适应异构的中间解码状态。因此需要一种自适应深度的方法来动态调整前瞻策略。

Method: AdaLook框架包含两个核心机制：(1) 基于候选分数方差动态决定是否继续前瞻展开，避免不必要的深层计算；(2) 当中间展开状态需要额外探索时支持分支扩展，允许解码器从信息丰富的中间状态重新触发前瞻。

Result: 在多个基准测试和不同模型上的实验表明，AdaLook在准确率与解码步数的权衡上优于现有的一步前瞻解码方法。

Conclusion: 自适应前瞻策略比固定的一步或深层前瞻更有效，能够根据解码状态的异质性动态调整探索深度，实现更好的计算效率与生成质量平衡。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models (DLMs) enable parallel text generation by iteratively refining masked tokens, offering a promising alternative to autoregressive decoding. Recent lookahead-based decoding methods improve the accuracy--efficiency trade-off by exploring future decoding states before committing token updates. However, existing approaches mainly rely on shallow one-step lookahead, which optimizes immediate information gain but can be suboptimal for longer-horizon decoding trajectories. Meanwhile, we find that a naive extension for deeper lookahead is also ineffective, as fixed-depth rollout introduces additional computation and cannot adapt to heterogeneous intermediate decoding states. Thus, in this work, we propose AdaLook, an adaptive lookahead framework for DLM decoding. AdaLook dynamically determines whether to continue rollout based on candidate-score variance and further enables branch expansion when intermediate rollout states require additional exploration. This design avoids unnecessary deep rollout while allowing the decoder to re-trigger lookahead from informative intermediate states. Experiments on various benchmarks and models demonstrate that AdaLook achieves a better accuracy--decoding steps trade-off than existing one-step lookahead decoding methods.

</details>


### [9] [DECODEM: Data Extraction from Corporate Organizational Documents via Enhanced Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15879)
*Jens Frankenreiter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了DECODEM——一组用于评估从组织文档中自动提取公司治理变量的基准数据集。通过对前沿大语言模型的系统评估，发现自动提取在法律条款上能达到高准确率，但不同变量间表现存在差异，且复杂的提示策略对前沿模型提升有限，但能缩小前沿模型与高效模型之间的差距。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建DECODEM基准数据集，包含随机抽样的公司章程和细则及其高质量人工标注；然后评估多种基于大语言模型的提取管道，这些管道在提示设计、任务分解和文档处理方式上存在差异；任务被转化为文档级二分类问题。

Conclusion: 前沿模型能够高精度地从复杂公司文档中提取具有法律意义的信息，自动特征提取在公司治理数据集构建中将发挥重要作用。管道设计可在一定程度上替代模型能力。

Abstract: Much empirical legal research depends on translating unstructured text into structured variables. In corporate governance research as elsewhere, this translation has traditionally relied on human coding of documents such as charters and bylaws, a process that is costly, difficult to scale, and often opaque. This paper introduces DECODEM, a set of benchmark datasets for evaluating the automated extraction of corporate governance variables from organizational documents. The benchmarks pair randomly sampled corporate charters and bylaws with high-quality human annotations covering a range of governance provisions commonly studied in empirical work.
  Using these datasets, the paper evaluates several large-language-model extraction pipelines that vary in prompt design, task decomposition, and document handling. The underlying task consists of a set of document-level binary classification problems, one for each governance variable. The results show that automated extraction is feasible at a high level of accuracy for many provisions, with median performance near the upper bound across approaches. At the same time, performance varies systematically across variables, with a small number of provisions accounting for most of the remaining errors. More elaborate prompting strategies and cascading pipelines do not consistently improve performance for frontier models, but substantially narrow the gap between frontier and efficiency-oriented models in some settings, suggesting that pipeline design can partly substitute for model capability.
  By providing a standardized benchmark and a systematic evaluation of extraction methods, the paper demonstrates that current frontier models can extract legally meaningful information from complex corporate documents with high accuracy and suggests an important future role for automated feature extraction in constructing corporate governance datasets.

### [10] [Better Starts, Better Ends: Bootstrapped Iterative Self-Reasoning Distillation for Compressed Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15736)
*Leichao Dong,Dongxu Zhang,Yiding Sun,Qirui Wang,Yuhan Wang,Lin Chen,Jihua Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出BIRD（自举式迭代自推理蒸馏）方法，通过两阶段蒸馏解决大推理模型在长链思维中的计算冗余问题。第一阶段通过简洁指令采样、过滤正确轨迹并进行提示切换微调，将简洁性内化为默认行为；第二阶段基于改进后的模型进行on-policy逆向KL蒸馏。在Qwen3系列上，BIRD显著提升了准确率-效率平衡，如Qwen3-8B在MATH-500上准确率从86.2%提升至92.0%，同时平均输出长度从3,099降至1,115 tokens。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大推理模型在长链思维（CoT）中产生大量冗余计算（重复验证、绕路等），而现有的on-policy自蒸馏方法存在初始化瓶颈——在冗长基模型产生的嘈杂前缀上施加KL损失，只能提供局部修正，学生仍会探索低效轨迹。

Method: BIRD两阶段蒸馏：（1）第一阶段：从基模型采样简洁解（加简洁指令），仅保留答案正确的轨迹，执行轻量级提示切换（prompt-switch）SFT，将指令诱导的简洁性转为默认行为模式；（2）第二阶段：基于预热后的模型，使用简洁自教师进行on-policy逆向KL蒸馏，此时蒸馏前缀更干净、信息更丰富。

Result: Qwen3系列上：MATH-500准确率从86.2%提升至92.0%，平均输出长度从3,099降至1,115 tokens；AIME基准也取得更优的准确率-效率权衡。优于单纯提示方法和冷启动on-policy蒸馏。

Conclusion: 前缀支持（prefix support）是高效推理蒸馏的核心因素。通过改善rollout分布再蒸馏，可突破初始化瓶颈，在保持高准确率的同时大幅减少推理开销。

Abstract: Large reasoning models often solve problems through long chain-of-thought (CoT) traces, yet much of this computation is spent on redundant derivations, repeated self-verification, and detours that do not improve the final answer. Existing on-policy self-distillation methods reduce this cost by matching a student model to a concise copy of itself on prefixes sampled from the student's own rollouts. We show that this objective has an initialization bottleneck. Since supervision is applied only to visited prefixes, training from a verbose base model places the KL loss on contexts that are often noisy, redundant, or already off track. In such regions, a concise teacher can provide only local corrections, while the student continues to explore trajectories that an efficient reasoner should avoid. In this paper, we propose BIRD(Bootstrapped Iterative Self-Reasoning Distillation), a two-stage self-reasoning distillation method that improves the rollout distribution before on-policy training. BIRD first samples concise solutions from the base model under a brevity instruction, keeps only answer-correct traces, and performs a lightweight prompt-switch SFT step. The traces are generated with the brevity instruction but learned under the original task prompt, turning instruction-induced conciseness into a default reasoning behavior. Starting from this warm model, BIRD then applies on-policy reverse-KL distillation with a concise self-teacher, now on cleaner and more informative prefixes. Across Qwen3 series models, BIRD achieves a stronger accuracy-efficiency trade-off than prompting and cold-start on-policy distillation on MATH-500 and AIME benchmarks. On Qwen3-8B, it improves MATH-500 accuracy from 86.2% to 92.0% while reducing the average response length from 3,099 to 1,115 tokens. These results highlight prefix support as a central factor in efficient reasoning distillation.

</details>


### [11] [Before the Action: Benchmarking LLMs on Prospective Hypothesis Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15766)
*Tianyun Zhong,Wangyi Jiang,Wei Wang,Xuanang Chen,Yaojie Lu,Shiwei Ye,Yuzhen Shi,Boyu Yang,Jinghang Wang,Han Li,Weiqi Zhai,Bing Zhao,Hu Wei,Haiyang Yu,Yongbin Li,Hongyu Lin,Le Sun,Xianpei Han*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出前瞻性假设发现（PHD）任务，评估LLM在开放、未得出结论的探索阶段自主构建假设空间的能力。为此构建了HypoArena基准（含988个案例的HypoData和HypoEval评估框架），实验表明前沿模型能力存在显著分层，且竞技场评估比绝对评分能更精细地区分模型差异。

Method: 提出PHD任务，构建HypoArena基准：1) HypoData通过"回顾性上下文回归"从已完成专家文档中重构结论前的上下文；2) HypoEval结合双向成对判断、Bradley-Terry-Davidson聚合排序和六维度评分标准。在15个前沿LLM上实验。

Result: 模型间存在显著能力分层，结构化分析技能对不同模型影响不同（低性能模型在HypoArena上提升，高性能模型反而下降）。竞技场评估比绝对评分更精细，聚合排序与人类专家及独立评判者高度一致。

Conclusion: PHD可作为评估LLM在结论未明时提出研究方向能力的独立目标，为衡量模型在科学发现前期的探索能力提供了新的视角和工具。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) excel at answering pre-specified questions, yet their ability to navigate the open-ended, pre-conclusion stage of discovery remains largely unmeasured. We introduce Prospective Hypothesis Discovery (PHD), which asks models to autonomously construct grounded, discriminative, and testable hypothesis spaces from inconclusive evidence, including anomalous observations and fragmented records, to guide subsequent investigation. To evaluate this capability, we introduce HypoArena, comprising HypoData, a benchmark of 988 cases across six scientific and analytical domains, and HypoEval, an evaluation framework for open-ended hypothesis sets. To construct HypoData at scale, we propose Retrospective Context Regression, a Forge--Audit pipeline that reconstructs pre-conclusion contexts from completed expert documents by removing explicit conclusions, target hypotheses, and retrospective causal attributions while preserving the factual substrate. Because PHD admits multiple valid outputs, HypoEval combines bidirectional pairwise judgments with Bradley--Terry--Davidson aggregation for ranking and six-dimensional rubric scoring for diagnosis. Experiments on 15 frontier LLMs reveal clear capability stratification and model-dependent effects of structured analytical skills, with gains for several lower-performing models on HypoArena but regressions for other systems, including a top-performing model. Compared with absolute rubric scoring, arena evaluation resolves finer-grained differences among models, with aggregated rankings showing strong agreement with human experts and an independent judge. Together, these results support treating PHD as a distinct target for evaluating how LLMs formulate investigative directions when final conclusions are withheld. Our code and data are publicly available at github.com/SKYLENAGE-AI/HypoArena and github.com/SKYLENAGE-AI/HypoArena.

### [12] [Cost-efficient generative AI summarization for scalable automated essay scoring in educational assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15829)
*Haowei Hua*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种生成式AI辅助摘要框架，利用GPT-5系列模型对长文本作文进行可控长度摘要，结合手工特征构建混合模型进行自动评分。实验表明GPT-5 mini评分一致性最高，GPT-5摘要质量最优，但高分段作文摘要质量下降，揭示了模型容量、摘要保真度与评估公平性之间的权衡。

Abstract: Automated essay scoring (AES) enables scalable assessment and timely feedback but remains challenged by transformer input-length limitations, which can cause information loss when processing long essays. This study proposes a generative AI-assisted summarization framework to improve long-form essay representation while maintaining scoring reliability. Using the ASAP 2.0 dataset, we generate controlled-length summaries with three GPT-5 variants (GPT-5, GPT-5 mini, and GPT-5 nano) and use them as inputs for downstream AES models. To preserve original writing signals, handcrafted linguistic features extracted from full essays are integrated with summary representations to form a hybrid framework. Summary quality decreases for higher-scoring essays, indicating that more complex writing is more difficult to compress without information loss. These findings reveal trade-offs among model capacity, summary fidelity, cost efficiency, and preservation of educational constructs. Overall, generative AI summarization offers a promising approach for scalable writing assessment while requiring careful validation of information preservation and fairness.

### [13] [CAMMAR: Culture-Aware Matryoshka for Metaphorical Arabic Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15847)
*Suzan Awinat,Alfonso Ortega del Puente*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出CAMMAR框架，通过嵌套的词汇、文化和隐喻嵌入子空间解决阿拉伯语模型中的"语义涂抹"问题，基于Al-Jurjani的nazum理论构建分阶段语义课程，实现无需训练的几何隐喻性度量。在词对齐的隐喻数据集上，几何读出在成对监督下检测隐喻效果显著（AUC达0.84），无监督时仅处于随机水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有阿拉伯语语言模型将词汇、文化和隐喻信息混杂在同一表征空间中（称为"语义涂抹"），无法区分这些不同层次的语义信息，阻碍了对阿拉伯语隐喻这一文化根植机制的准确理解与建模。

Method: 提出CAMMAR框架：1) 基于Al-Jurjani的nazum理论设计嵌套的词汇、文化、隐喻三层嵌入子空间；2) 采用分阶段语义课程学习（staged semantic curriculum）；3) 通过词汇层与隐喻层表示之间的距离定义无需训练的几何隐喻性度量；4) 通过词对齐的比喻/字面配对数据进行成对监督训练。

Result: 在词对齐的阿拉伯语隐喻数据集上：1) 有监督条件下几何隐喻性检测AUC达0.84，82.6%的比喻对中比喻表达优于字面表达；2) 无监督领域对比下仅处于随机水平；3) 词汇层基于形态词根作为锚点带来小幅但一致的性能提升。

Conclusion: CAMMAR通过分层语义表征有效区分了阿拉伯语的隐喻与字面意义，揭示了"有监督可解读"与"无监督不涌现"的清晰边界，验证了将形态词根作为测量锚点的有效性。工作将开源数据集、文化概念清单和代码。

Abstract: Metaphor in Arabic is a culturally grounded mechanism for constructing meaning, encoding cultural knowledge that shapes interpretation. Yet current Arabic language models typically collapse lexical, cultural, and metaphorical information into a single representational space, a phenomenon we term "semantic smearing". We introduce CAMMAR (Culture-Aware Matryoshka for Metaphorical Arabic Representations), a representation learning framework that organizes meaning into nested lexical, cultural, and metaphorical embedding subspaces through a staged semantic curriculum. The design implements compositional principles of Al-Jurjani's theory of nazum, modeling figurative meaning as compositionally grounded in prior semantic relations, and yields a training-free geometric measure of metaphoricity based on the distance between lexical and metaphorical representations.
  Evaluated on a new span-annotated Arabic metaphor set as word-matched figurative/literal pairs, the geometric readout detects metaphor well above chance when the inter-layer geometry is shaped by paired supervision (AUC up to 0.84; figurative outscores its literal counterpart for the same word in 82.6\% of pairs), but sits at chance under an unsupervised domain contrast alone, a clean separation between a legible-under-supervision regime and a non-emergent one. A controlled ablation shows that grounding the lexical layer in morphological roots gives a small but consistent gain, an effect absent from direct probing that reflects the layer's quality as a measurement anchor. We will release the datasets, cultural concept inventory, and code upon acceptance.

### [14] [Contextual Semantic Relevance Tracks fMRI BOLD Responses During Naturalistic Speech Comprehension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15856)
*Kun Sun,Rong Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究分析两个fMRI数据集，发现语义相关性（单词与近期语义上下文的关联程度）比概率性惊讶度（surprisal）更稳健地预测自然语言理解过程中的BOLD反应，表明fMRI对语境语义整合更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然语言理解中，惊讶度（surprisal）虽被广泛用于量化局部单词的不可预期性，但其能否稳健预测fMRI BOLD信号一直存在争议。作者试图寻找更有效的神经指标。

Method: 分析Alice和Moth两个公开fMRI数据集，使用广义加性混合模型（GAMMs）处理转换后的BOLD响应，并用FIR/去卷积分析测试原始连续BOLD时间序列。

Result: 在Alice数据集中，语义相关性在全部12个ROI中显著，而惊讶度经FDR校正后不显著；在Moth数据集中，语义相关性在全部30个ROI中呈现一致的负向效应，惊讶度无类似模式。

Conclusion: 语义相关性是衡量语境语义契合度的有效BOLD敏感指标；fMRI对语境语义整合更敏感，而局部概率预测误差更难被可靠检测；语义相关性将语言理解计算模型从单纯预测扩展至语境敏感的语义整合。

Abstract: Naturalistic language comprehension requires listeners to process both local probabilistic expectations and contextual semantic relations. Surprisal has been widely used to quantify local word unexpectedness, but evidence that it robustly predicts fMRI BOLD responses during continuous comprehension has been mixed. This study investigates whether contextual semantic relevance, defined as how strongly an incoming word relates to its recent semantic context, predicts BOLD responses during naturalistic speech comprehension. We analyzed two public fMRI datasets, the Alice dataset and the Moth dataset, treating them as complementary rather than identical replications. Transformed BOLD responses were modeled with generalized additive mixed models (GAMMs) and original continuous BOLD time series were tested with FIR/deconvolution analyses. In Alice, semantic relevance was significant across all 12 ROIs (region of interest), whereas surprisal was not significant after FDR correction. In Moth, semantic relevance showed consistent negative effects across all 30 ROIs, while surprisal showed no comparable pattern. These findings suggest that semantic relevance is a promising BOLD-sensitive metric of contextual semantic fit. More broadly, our findings support the view that slow hemodynamic responses during naturalistic speech comprehension may be especially sensitive to contextual semantic integration, whereas local probabilistic prediction error may be more difficult to detect reliably with fMRI. In this sense, semantic relevance extends computational models of language comprehension from prediction alone toward context-sensitive semantic integration.

### [15] [Conditional Reliability of Toxicity Signals for Multilingual and Code-Mixed Abuse Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15861)
*Indraveni Chebolu,Rohan Singh,Arnab Mallick,Harmesh Rana*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 论文提出ToxGate，一种条件信任融合机制，用于在印度多语言和代码混合短文本中，根据语境条件性地利用外部毒性工具信号，显著提升了高风险内容（如显式辱骂、暴力威胁等）的检测效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的审核系统依赖外部毒性工具，但这些工具在面对代码混合、音译、俚语和语言不匹配时不可靠。论文旨在解决如何在不完全信任这些工具的前提下，有条件地利用其信号来提高审核可靠性。

Method: 提出ToxGate，一种信任融合头（trust-fusion head），它根据编码器表示对每个辅助信号进行条件化处理，再将信号加入预测状态。通过门控机制实现源特定（source-specific）的条件融合。

Result: 在三个短文本滥用数据集、四种Transformer编码器和五种随机种子设置下，ToxGate在12个域内设置中提升10个，在8个迁移设置中提升7个。最大的可解释增益出现在高风险审核切片中，包括显式辱骂、暴力威胁和跨数据集迁移。

Conclusion: 审核系统应将外部毒性工具和先验视为条件性证据而非固定特征或地面真相。源特定门控在迁移、严重滥用切片和高风险分类中效果最强。

Abstract: Moderation systems increasingly rely on external toxicity tools, but those tools are unreliable under code-mixing, transliteration, slang, and language mismatch. We study the \emph{conditional reliability} of toxicity priors in Indian multilingual and code-mixed short text: English toxicity, Indic abuse, and rule-based severity cues can be useful evidence, but only in some linguistic and abuse-severity contexts. We propose ToxGate, a trust-fusion head that conditions each auxiliary signal on the encoder representation before adding it to the prediction state. Across three short-text abuse datasets, four transformer encoders, and five seeds per setting, ToxGate improves over matched plain encoders in 10 of 12 in-domain settings and 7 of 8 transfer settings. The largest and most interpretable gains occur in high-risk moderation slices, including explicit slurs, violent threats, and cross-dataset transfer. The broader lesson is that moderation systems should treat external toxicity tools and priors as conditional evidence rather than fixed features or ground truth, in focused ablations, source-specific gating gives the strongest results in transfer, severe-abuse slices, and high-risk triage.

</details>


### [16] [An MLIR-Based Compilation Method for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15865)
*Pengchao Hu,Zhibin Xin,Yifan Chen,Yangyang Zhou,Liang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于MLIR的大语言模型编译方法，通过TopOp和TpuOp两个算子方言，将模型从高层语义表示逐层lower到目标硬件表示，并针对Transformer推理循环设计了三段式静态编译策略（prefill、prefill_kv、decode），已在TPU-MLIR编译器和LLM-TPU部署项目中实现，支持多种生成式模型和量化形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型已成为AI加速器的主导负载，但在专用硬件上部署仍面临两大核心挑战：如何将训练好的模型导入编译器友好的中间表示，以及如何在有限的片上内存下高效调度自回归推理循环。

Method: 基于MLIR的编译方法，设计了两个算子方言：TopOp（高层图方言，与源框架和目标芯片无关，表达模型语义）和TpuOp（目标硬件方言，承载量化、层分组、内存布局等芯片相关决策）。模型先表示为TopOp，逐层lower到TpuOp，最终生成可部署的二进制文件。每个Transformer层被分为三个阶段进行静态编译：prefill、prefill_kv（带历史KV缓存的prefill）、decode，以适应提示并行处理和逐token生成的不同计算特性。

Result: 该方法已在TPU-MLIR编译器和LLM-TPU部署项目中实现，支持Qwen、Llama、InternVL、MiniCPM-V等多种生成式模型，以及GPTQ、AWQ、AutoRound等多种量化和部署形式。

Conclusion: 本文提出的两级方言设计和三段式编译策略有效解决了LLM在专用硬件上的部署难题，实现了从训练模型到目标硬件的端到端编译流程，具有良好的框架无关性和硬件适配性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have become the dominant workload on modern AI accelerators, yet deploying them on specialized hardware still faces two core challenges: how to import a trained model into a compiler-friendly intermediate representation, and how to efficiently schedule the autoregressive inference loop under limited on-chip memory. This paper presents an MLIR (Multi-Level Intermediate Representation) based compilation method for large language models, illustrated using two dialects of operators, TopOp and TpuOp. TopOp serves as a high-level graph dialect that is independent of both the source framework and the target chip, and is responsible for expressing model semantics; TpuOp serves as the target hardware dialect, carrying chip-related decisions such as quantization, layer groups, and memory layout. A model is first represented as TopOp, then lowered layer by layer to TpuOp, and finally a deployable binary is generated. In addition, each Transformer layer is split into three stages for static compilation: prefill, prefill_kv (prefill with historical key-value cache), and decode, so as to accommodate the different computational characteristics of prompt-parallel processing and per-token generation. The method has been implemented in the TPU-MLIR compiler{https://github.com/sophgo/tpu-mlir} and the LLM-TPU deployment project\footnote{https://github.com/sophgo/LLM-TPU}, supporting a variety of generative models including the Qwen, Llama, InternVL, and MiniCPM-V series, as well as multiple quantization and deployment forms such as GPTQ, AWQ, and AutoRound.

### [17] [How Much Human Label Variation Does Formal Semantic Structure Explain?: Group-Level Effects and Item-Level Ceilings in NLI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15870)
*Haram Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过ChaosNLI数据集，量化形式语义结构对自然语言推理中标注变异的影响，发现其仅能解释3.3-3.6%的熵方差，且不改变分歧内容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管标注变异日益被视为信号而非噪声，但形式语义结构在多大程度上解释这种变异从未被直接测量过。

Method: 使用基于规则的算子和单调性标注器（在MED上验证），对ChaosNLI中3,113个SNLI和MNLI项目进行三项预注册分析，包括边界、上限和组成不变性检验。

Result: （1）非纯向上单调的假设标注熵显著更高（Cliff's delta = -0.284）；（2）形式语义仅解释3.3-3.6%的熵方差，AUC仅0.606；（3）组成不变性检验全为null结果。

Conclusion: 形式语义结构仅小幅改变标注者分歧程度，未显著改变分歧内容。

Abstract: Human label variation in natural language inference is increasingly treated as signal rather than noise, but how much of it formal semantic structure explains has not been measured directly. We measure it on the 3,113 SNLI and MNLI items of ChaosNLI, using a rule-based operator and monotonicity tagger validated against MED (0.883 agreement at the edit site, 0.807 on the sentence-level summary our analyses consume), three preregistered analysis blocks, and full reporting of negative results. Three bounds emerge. First, a group-level boundary: hypotheses that are not purely upward monotone show reliably higher label entropy (Cliff's delta = -0.284), and rank-based tests defend the effect against operator-presence and length reductions, though a bounded-outcome sensitivity check weakens the regression form of the length defense. Second, an item-level ceiling: the same formal profiles explain only 3.3 to 3.6 percent of entropy variance and reach a median-split AUC of 0.606, too weak to identify high-disagreement items. Third, composition invariance: across the boundary, three high-powered preregistered contrasts on validated error shares and explanation-type shares (VariErr, LiTEx) all return null results. In this sample, formal semantic structure shifts how much annotators disagree by a small amount and does not detectably change what they disagree about. ChaosNLI-S/M consists of items selected for low original agreement, and every claim is conditioned on that scope. All analyses were preregistered in a version-controlled research log, whose audit trail, including one corrected interpretation rule, the paper discloses.

### [18] [Induction in Both Directions: A Mechanistic Analysis of In-Context Learning in Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15893)
*Andy Catruna,Emilian Radoi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了扩散语言模型（DLM）如何实现归纳（induction）机制，发现DLM学习到一种双向归纳电路，能够利用过去和未来的上下文信息进行复制，并且在没有显式时间步嵌入的情况下，隐式地计算全局掩码比例作为时间步信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归Transformer的内部机制已被广泛研究，但扩散语言模型（DLM）作为新兴的文本生成方法，其内部工作机制尚不明确。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索DLM如何实现归纳这一在上下文学习中至关重要的机制。

Method: 通过对比架构匹配的仅注意力自回归模型（AR）和吸收掩码扩散语言模型（DLM），研究两者在归纳机制上的差异。分析了前文头、后文头和归纳头在残差流中的信息写入与读取过程，以及双向上下文对归纳能力的影响。

Result: DLM学习到一种方向对称的双向归纳电路，能利用过去和未来的上下文。仅在左上下文可见时，DLM的归纳能力不优于AR模型；但当掩码标记两侧上下文均可见时，DLM表现出更强的归纳能力。此外，DLM隐式地计算全局掩码比例作为时间步信号。

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型通过双向归纳电路实现上下文学习，其优势来源于双向上下文访问而非更强的单向机制。同时，DLM展现出隐式利用全局掩码比例作为时间步信息的计算能力。

Abstract: While the internal mechanisms of autoregressive (AR) transformers have been studied extensively, much less is known about diffusion language models (DLMs), an emerging alternative that generates text by iterative denoising. In this work, we study how DLMs implement induction, a mechanism behind in-context learning in which the model finds a repeated context and copies the token that followed it. Our analysis compares attention-only AR models and absorbing-mask DLMs with matched architectures. We find that DLMs learn a bidirectional induction circuit, where previous-token and next-token heads write local context into the residual stream and later induction heads use it to find and copy the answer from the matching source position. The circuit is direction-symmetric, working whether the source appears in the past or in the future. When only left context is visible, matching what an AR model sees, the DLM does not outperform its AR counterpart in induction capabilities. However, we observe it has stronger induction when both sides of the masked token are visible, pointing to bidirectional context access rather than a stronger one-sided mechanism. Beyond induction, we provide causal evidence that DLMs compute the global fraction of masked tokens and use it as an implicit timestep, even though they are given no explicit timestep embedding.

Method: 本文是一篇观点论文，通过理论分析和批判性思考，指出现有自我解释评估协议在合理性和忠实性方面的缺陷，并提出扩展评估维度到可操作性的建议。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate natural language explanations that rationalize their own decisions, a phenomenon commonly referred to as self-explanations.Such explanations have emerged as a promising direction for explainable artificial intelligence (XAI), particularly for interpreting LLM behavior.However, while self-explanations often appear plausible, whether they faithfully reflect a model's underlying reasoning process remains an open question. In this opinion paper, we argue that self-explanations can be highly plausible, questionably faithful, and yet highly actionable. From a traditional XAI perspective, we identify the limitations of standard evaluation protocols for LLM-generated self-explanations and propose practical guidelines for assessing their plausibility and faithfulness. Moreover, we argue that evaluation should extend beyond these criteria to actionability, highlighting applications of LLM rationalization capabilities that support informed decision-making and appropriate action across diverse stakeholders.

### [20] [BayesPO: Bayesian Prompt Optimization via Parallel-Tempered Gradient-Guided Discrete MCMC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16001)
*Junjie Zhou,Zhijian Ou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出BayesPO框架，将提示优化视为贝叶斯后验采样问题，利用梯度引导的离散MCMC方法（Gibbs-with-Langevin + 并行回火）在词汇表上进行采样，实验显示在24个指令归纳子任务上准确率提升约3%，但存在过拟合和计算成本高的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动提示优化器多为启发式搜索过程，缺乏概率基础。作者希望将提示优化建模为贝叶斯后验采样，从而提供更原则性的优化框架。

Method: 将提示优化定义为结合任务似然（奖励解释输入-输出示例的提示）与语言模型先验（偏好流畅指令）的后验分布，转化为基于能量的采样问题。采用Metropolis-Hastings校正的Gibbs-with-Langevin (GwL)提议，并结合并行回火策略应对LLM能量景观的崎岖性，同时针对不等权重的LLM嵌入进行适配。

Result: 在Qwen2.5模型上：1) 诊断任务中发现了语义有意义的提示；2) 并行回火帮助跳出了诗歌补全任务的局部最优；3) 在24个指令归纳子任务上，后优化APE提示的平均准确率从60.04%提升至63.23%。

Conclusion: 贝叶斯提示采样可作为有原则的后优化工具，但存在两个主要局限性：能量最小化可能过拟合小规模优化集，且当前采样器计算成本较高。该方向为概率提示优化提供了有前景的思路。

Abstract: Prompt optimization adapts large language models (LLMs) without updating model parameters, but many automatic prompt optimizers remain heuristic search procedures over candidate instructions. This paper studies prompt optimization as Bayesian posterior sampling over discrete prompt tokens. We define a posterior distribution by combining a task likelihood term, which rewards prompts that explain input-output examples, with a language-model prior, which favors fluent instructions. This converts prompt optimization into an energy-based posterior sampling problem, for which gradients can be used to guide discrete Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) proposals over vocabulary tokens. We refer to our framework as BayesPO, short for Bayesian Prompt Optimization. In this paper, BayesPO is instantiated with Markov chain Monte Carlo: it uses a Metropolis-Hastings corrected Gibbs-with-Langevin (GwL) proposal and integrates parallel tempering for global exploration of rugged LLM-induced energy landscapes. The concrete sampler further adapts the GwL sampler to the practical constraints of non-weight-tied LLM embeddings. Experiments with Qwen2.5 models show that the sampler discovers semantically meaningful prompts on diagnostic tasks, that parallel tempering helps escape a local optimum in a poetry completion task, and that post-optimizing APE prompts on 24 instruction-induction subtasks improves average accuracy from 60.04% to 63.23%. The study also reveals two main limitations: energy minimization may overfit small optimization sets, and the current sampler remains computationally expensive. These findings position Bayesian prompt sampling as a principled post-optimization tool and point to a promising direction for probabilistic prompt optimization.

</details>

### [24] [Frontier Language Models Struggle to Copy: Text Can Be Better Viewed in 2D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16072)
*Haodong Wen,Yiran Zhang,Yingfa Chen,Kaifeng Lyu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现即使最先进的大语言模型也无法完美执行简单的输入字符串复制任务，归因于Transformer位置编码的归纳偏差。作者提出2D-RoPE，将文本组织成2D网格，通过固定列偏移实现复制，在合成实验和规模化预训练中均展现出显著优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿LLM能解决复杂推理问题，却连简单的输入字符串复制（在上下文窗口内）都无法完美完成。作者将此归因于Transformer位置编码的归纳偏差——它倾向于通过匹配局部上下文来复制，而非精确定位输入位置，这暴露了现有架构在基础操作上的根本缺陷。

Method: 提出2D-RoPE，将文本从1D序列组织为2D网格，每个token分配行ID和列ID。复制任务简化为在固定列偏移下检索输入token，使任务易于学习。在合成复制实验和DCLM大规模预训练（最高1.4B参数）中验证。

Result: 浅层Transformer结合2D-RoPE在合成复制实验中实现完美复制，输入长度远超训练时数百倍；而标准位置编码显著落后。在DCLM大规模预训练中，2D-RoPE语言模型在复制任务上的优势在1.4B参数规模下一致成立。

Conclusion: 将文本视为2D结构有益于语言建模，复制只是2D位置编码优势的一个体现。作者希望该工作能激励未来进一步探索2D位置编码的潜力。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) can solve advanced reasoning problems in seconds, we show that even frontier models fail to perform a much simpler operation: exactly copying an input string that lies well within their context windows. We attribute this failure to positional encodings in Transformer architectures, whose inductive bias favors copying through a shortcut based on matching local contexts rather than carefully locating the corresponding input positions. To address this issue, we introduce 2D-RoPE, which organizes text into a 2D grid rather than a 1D sequence and assigns each token a row ID and a column ID. Under this view, copying becomes simply retrieving input tokens at a fixed column offset, which makes the task easy to learn. In synthetic copy experiments, shallow Transformers with 2D-RoPE achieve perfect copying at input lengths hundreds of times longer than those seen during training, whereas standard positional encodings fall far behind. We further show that the advantage of 2D-RoPE language models on copy tasks consistently holds in large-scale pretraining on DCLM with model sizes up to 1.4B parameters. Overall, our results suggest that viewing text in 2D can benefit language modeling, and we hope this encourages future work to further explore the potential of 2D positional encodings.

</details>


### [25] [Controlling Implicit Shortcut Reliance in L2 Spoken English Auto-markers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16085)
*Shilin Gao,Mark J. F. Gales,Kate M. Knill*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的训练准则，旨在减少语言能力评估系统中分类器对"捷径"特征的过度依赖，从而防止考生通过利用这些捷径而非提升真实能力来获取高分。在基于音频和语音识别文本的两种评估系统上，该方法成功将模型与可被利用特征的关联度降低至接近人类参考水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语音和语言处理任务直接使用原始音频或文本作为输入，基于Transformer等复杂模型的系统容易学习到"捷径"——过度依赖输入的特定方面来产生输出。在语言能力评估中，这种过度依赖使得学习者可以通过利用捷径而非真正提升能力来提高分数，形成作弊风险。

Method: 提出一种新颖的训练准则（modified training criterion），通过修改损失函数或训练目标，减少分类器对可被利用特征的依赖。该方法在两种评估系统上验证：一种基于音频输入，另一种基于语音识别文本输入。

Result: 1) 两种系统均显示出与可被利用特征的关联度高于人类参考，表明存在过度依赖；2) 引入修改后的训练准则后，这种关联度降低至更接近人类参考水平。

Conclusion: 所提出的训练准则能有效减少语言能力评估系统对捷径特征的过度依赖，限制了通过利用系统漏洞进行作弊的可能性，提升了评估的公平性和可靠性。

Abstract: Increasingly, speech and language processing tasks take either audio or text directly rather than extracting features from these as the input to the classifier or regressor. Often these systems make use of complex, for example transformer-based, processes that have the ability to derive highly non-linear mappings between the input and the output. Unfortunately these systems can also learn ''shortcuts'' where the classifier is overly reliant on particular aspects of the input to yield the output. For the task of language proficiency assessment, this over-reliance can enable learners to increase their score by exploiting the shortcut rather than improving their ability. This paper introduces a novel training criterion that is able to reduce the classifier's reliance on shortcuts, thus for example limiting this option for malpractice in language assessment. This process is illustrated on two forms of assessment system, one based on the audio the other on the speech recognition text. The results show that, for both systems, there is higher correlations with features that could be exploited for malpractice than expected from the human reference, indicating an over-reliance on these features. By introducing the modified training criterion, this correlation can be reduced to be closer to the reference correlation.

</details>


### [26] [Rate-Utility Frontiers for Language Encodings: Comparing Tokens, Bytes, and Pixels Under Controlled Linguistic Content](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16117)
*Ingo Ziegler,Martin Krebs,Desmond Elliott*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过控制内容与下游容量，比较了子词token、原始字节和渲染像素三种编码方式在13种语言、5种文字下的率-效用边界，发现没有一种编码在所有任务和容量下占优：像素保留表面形式最佳，字节保留跨语言对齐最佳（尤其同文字多语言场景），token支持主题分类最佳。编码选择取决于任务、语言组合、容量和计算预算的率-效用权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常在不同建模约束下比较不同编码方式，使得不同语言暴露的语言内容量不同。作者希望控制内容和下游容量，公平比较不同编码方式在相同条件下真正保留了哪些信息。

Method: 使用13种语言、5种文字的平行句，通过共享瓶颈（瓶颈宽度从低到高扫描）比较token、bytes、pixels三种编码，绘制率-效用边界曲线，分离了输入位置数、编码后潜在容量、压缩后任务相关信息三个常被混淆的量。

Result: 1. 没有编码在所有任务和容量下占优；2. 像素保留表面形式最好，字节保留跨语言对齐最好（尤其同文字），token支持主题分类最好；3. 序列长度本身不能解释这些差异——短输入可能丢弃有用信息，长输入可能保留易压缩信息。

Conclusion: 编码选择不是对token、bytes或pixels的固定偏好，而是取决于任务、语言组合、容量和计算预算的率-效用权衡。

Abstract: Language models encode text as subword tokens, raw bytes, or rendered pixels, but these encodings are usually compared under modeling constraints that expose different amounts of linguistic content to models across different languages. We instead ask what each encoding preserves when both the content and the downstream capacity are controlled. Using verified parallel sentences across thirteen languages and five scripts, we compare tokens, bytes, and pixels through a shared bottleneck whose width is swept to trace rate-utility frontiers. This separates three quantities that are often conflated: the number of input positions an encoding creates, the latent capacity available after encoding, and the task-relevant information that survives compression. We evaluate three utilities: surface form preservation, cross-lingual sentence alignment, and topic classification. No encoding dominates across tasks or capacity regimes. Pixels preserve surface form best, bytes preserve cross-lingual alignment best, especially in same-script multilingual settings, and tokens support topic prediction best. These performances are not explained by sequence length alone. Short inputs can discard useful meaning, while long inputs can preserve information that compresses well. Choosing an encoding is therefore not a fixed preference for tokens, bytes, or pixels, but a rate-utility tradeoff that depends on the task, language mix, capacity regime, and compute budget.

</details>


### [27] [ToolSciVer: Multimodal Scientific Claim Verification with Visual Tool Augmented Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16131)
*Binglin Zhou,Peng Shi,Ryo Kamoi,Nan Zhang,Rui Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ToolSciVer 是首个工具增强的多模态科学声明验证框架，通过为视觉语言模型配备三种类型感知工具（表格行列聚焦、图表结构解析、高分辨率区域缩放），并利用GRPO强化学习策略优化工具使用，在多个数据集上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态科学声明验证方法难以定位关键视觉证据、准确解读结构化科学图表，以及将多模态观测整合为可靠推理，导致验证效果不佳。

Method: 提出 ToolSciVer 框架，为VLM配备三种类型感知视觉工具（表格行列聚焦、图表结构解析、高分辨率区域缩放），将密集科学视觉内容转化为面向声明的显式证据，并使用GRPO结合复合奖励（答案正确性、格式有效性、长度控制、工具使用效率、工具有效性惩罚）进行策略训练。

Result: 在 SciVer 和 MuSciClaims 数据集上，基于 Qwen、InternVL、Gemma 三个模型家族的五个VLM进行实验，ToolSciVer 相比四种竞争基线（包括基于提示和基于RL的工具使用方法）取得了更优性能。

Conclusion: 学习到的类型感知工具使用策略对于科学声明验证任务非常有效，ToolSciVer 框架为该领域提供了新的有效范式。

Abstract: Multimodal Scientific Claim Verification (MSCV) requires models to verify scientific claims using visually grounded evidence from papers, including figures, tables, charts, and textual context. However, existing methods often fail because they struggle to locate decisive visual evidence, accurately read structured scientific visuals, and integrate multimodal observations into reliable reasoning. We introduce ToolSciVer, the first tool-augmented framework for MSCV to our knowledge. ToolSciVer equips a VLM with three type-aware visual tools, table row/column focus, chart-to-structure parsing, and high-resolution region zoom, which convert dense scientific visuals into explicit, claim-facing evidence, and trains the policy with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) under a composite reward of answer correctness, format validity, length control, tool-use efficiency, and tool-validity penalties. Experiments on SciVer and MuSciClaims datasets on five VLMs from three model families (Qwen, InternVL, Gemma) demonstrate that our method achieves superior performance compared to four competitive baselines including prompting-based and RL-based tool-use methods, highlighting the effectiveness of learned, type-aware tool use for scientific claim verification.

</details>

### [28] [Consistent pricing of bivariate interest rate exotics via constrained Schrödinger optimal transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15952)
*Patrick Roome*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于Schrödinger最优传输对偶拉格朗日方法的建模框架，用于在CMS利差期权与两个底层CMS期权市场之间保持一致性，实现双变量利率奇异期权的定价与无套利边界计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMS利差期权与其底层CMS期权市场之间存在内在关联，但现有方法难以在三个相互关联的市场间保持定价一致性，且缺乏有效的无套利边界计算工具。

Method: 通过求解受约束Schrödinger最优传输问题的对偶拉格朗日形式，建立一个同时拟合三个市场（CMS利差期权及两个底层CMS期权）的建模框架。

Result: 通过具体数值算例展示了该框架在定价方法论和无套利边界计算两方面的实际可行性。

Conclusion: 该方法为复杂利率衍生品提供了稳健的定价工具，能确保与流动性市场工具的一致性。

Abstract: We develop a modeling framework for pricing bivariate interest rate exotic derivatives that maintains consistency across three interconnected markets: CMS spread options and the two underlying CMS option markets that define the spread. Our approach also enables the computation of no-arbitrage bounds for exotic derivatives given observable market prices in the spread option and underlying CMS option markets. The method relies on solving the dual Lagrangian of a constrained version of the Shrödinger optimal transport problem and we demonstrate the practical applicability of our framework through concrete numerical examples that illustrate both the pricing methodology and the computation of no-arbitrage bounds. The approach offers a robust tool for pricing complex interest rate derivatives while ensuring consistency with liquid market instruments.

### [29] [Equilibrium analysis in a multi-agent reinsurance chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15962)
*Kaizheng Wang,Wei Liu,Zhuo Jin,Wenyuan Wa*

Main category: q-fin.MF

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含m家保险公司和n家再保险公司的多层再保险链随机微分博弈模型，运用Stackelberg博弈刻画各层级的战略互动，并分别分析了比例再保险和超额损失再保险两种合约下的均衡投资与再保险策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中的再保险市场呈现多层链条结构，且存在上下游保险公司与再保险公司之间的战略竞争与合作，现有研究缺乏对这一多层博弈结构的统一建模分析。

Method: 采用Stackelberg微分博弈建模再保险链各层级买卖双方的交互，非零和博弈模型刻画保险公司间的竞争行为；运用动态规划与博弈论结合，求解扩展的HJB系统，在均值-方差准则下推导封闭形式的均衡策略。

Result: 保险市场竞争加剧会导致再保险链各层级合约的安全附加保费（safety loadings）下降。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多层再保险链中竞争强度与再保险定价之间的传导机制，为不同再保险合约类型（比例再保险与超额损失再保险）下的投资与再保险决策提供了理论依据。

Abstract: This paper investigates a multi-layer reinsurance chain within a stochastic differential game framework involving m competing insurers and n reinsurers. Specifically, Stackelberg differential games are employed to characterize the strategic interactions between reinsurance buyers and sellers at each layer of the chain. In addition, a non-zero-sum game model is established to capture the competitive behavior among insurers. Both insurers and reinsurers are allowed to invest in a risk-free asset and a risky asset. To examine the heterogeneity of reinsurance chains under different contract types, the analysis is conducted separately for proportional reinsurance and excess-of-loss reinsurance. By combining dynamic programming and game theory, closed-form equilibrium strategies for investment and reinsurance are derived by solving the extended Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman (HJB) systems under the mean-variance (MV) criterion. Numerical analysis is conducted to explore the impact of key parameters on the equilibrium strategies. The results indicate that intensified competition in the insurance market leads to a reduction in the safety loadings of reinsurance contracts at each layer of the reinsurance chain.

### [30] [On the Effectiveness of Fact Checking Information from Politically Congruent and Incongruent Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15364)
*Jiangen He,Benjamin D Horne,Dorit Nevo*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文通过两项实验（n=705）发现，意识形态配置的LLM聊天机器人能显著改变用户对真假新闻标题的信任度，即使机器人政治立场与用户不一致。当机器人错误或给出不确定答案时，也会显著影响信任度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体平台从人工事实核查转向嵌入对话式LLM聊天机器人，但LLM可通过回复内容、引用来源和配置人设进行意识形态定制，这与人工核查员存在本质差异。需要研究这种意识形态配置如何影响用户对事实核查信息的反应。

Method: 采用两项被试内实验（n=705），通过操纵LLM聊天机器人的意识形态配置（政治立场、引用来源、人设），测量用户对真假政治新闻标题的信任度变化。

Result: 1. LLM事实核查能显著改变用户对真假新闻的信任度，即使政治立场不一致；2. 政治一致性仅在处理政治距离远的标题时影响信任度提升；3. 政治一致性不影响对假新闻的信任降低效果；4. 当LLM给出错误或不确定答案时，同样显著改变用户信任。

Conclusion: LLM具备大规模纠正虚假信息的潜力，但也存在大规模污染真实信息的风险。意识形态配置对事实核查效果的影响是有限的——并非在所有场景中都起作用，但错误或不确切的回复仍然具有影响力。

Abstract: Social media companies have shifted away from human fact-checkers and instead have embedded conversational Large Language Models (LLM) on their platforms. LLM chatbots differ from human fact-checkers in many ways that may shape user responses to corrections. Of particular interest in this study is that LLM chatbots can be ideologically configured via the content emphasized in their responses, the sources cited, and the configured persona. Using data from two within-subjects experiments (n=705), this paper investigates the effectiveness of fact checking information from ideologically configured LLM chatbots. We find that LLM fact-checkers significantly shift trust in true and false political news headlines, even when the chatbot is politically incongruent with the user. The perceived political congruency between the participant and the bot matters only when headlines are politically distant. That is, trust in correctly labeled true headlines increases less when politically distant chatbots check distant headlines and increases more when moderate chatbots check distant headlines. The perceived political congruency of LLM chatbots did not impact their effectiveness at decreasing trust in false headlines. Unfortunately, LLM fact-checkers also significantly change trust in news when they are wrong or provide inconclusive answers. Our results demonstrate both the potential for LLMs to correct false information at scale but also their potential to taint the truth at scale.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Electronic health record audit logs record timestamped actions through which clinical work is carried out. This Perspective explains that breadth by articulating audit logs as multi-axial event streams and drawing implications for representation learning, evaluation, and governance. This structure motivates foundation-model pretraining to learn reusable representations over the raw stream. Reading audit logs as multi-axial traces specifies what such representations must preserve, how their value should be tested, and how their use should be governed.

Abstract: Human mobility data have become fundamental to research across transportation, public health, urban science, and disaster resilience. Here we present Complete Trip, a mobility dataset that reconstructs linked multimodal travel behavior from passively collected smartphone location-based services (LBS) data. The first released implementation covers six counties in Utah throughout 2020 and represents journeys across car, bus, rail, and active transportation through a four-stage workflow consisting of trip identification, mode imputation, route reconstruction, and trip linking. Complete Trip preserves journey-level relationships by linking sequential travel segments where multiple segments belong to the same travel episode, provides network-based route representations on digital transportation networks, and supports population-level analyses through statistically calibrated expansion weights. ### [33] [The CRAFT principles for the responsible use of large language models in policymaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15704)
*Willem Fourie,Gray Manicom,Tanya de Villiers-Botha*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大语言模型在政策制定中的应用潜力与风险，并提出了CRAFT原则（控制、严谨、问责、公平、透明）来平衡效益与风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 政策制定者面临如何合理利用人工智能（尤其是大语言模型）改进政策制定过程的挑战，需要在发挥其优势的同时防范潜在风险。

Method: 提出CRAFT原则框架——控制（Control）、严谨（Rigour）、问责（Accountability）、公平（Fairness）和透明（Transparency），以指导大语言模型在政策制定中的负责任使用。

Result: 大语言模型可增强政策相关信息收集、解读、综合及政策文件起草能力，但存在输出看似合理但不一定正确、训练数据代表性不足导致偏见、敏感信息泄露及长期依赖和技能退化等风险。

Conclusion: 遵循CRAFT原则有助于在政策制定中最大化大语言模型的效用，同时有效管理相关风险，维护公众信任。

Abstract: Policymakers around the world face the question of how to use artificial intelligence in general, and large language models in particular, to improve the policymaking process. Used well, large language models can strengthen the collection, interpretation and synthesis of policy-relevant information and the drafting of policy-relevant output. Yet the use of large language models in policymaking is associated with risks. Output that is plausible but not necessarily correct, bias resulting from unrepresentative training data, the exposure of sensitive information and, over time, deskilling and dependency can erode trust if large language models are not used thoughtfully. The CRAFT principles - control, rigour, accountability, fairness and transparency - offer a way to make the most of large language models in policymaking while managing the risks.

</details>


### [34] [EduGuard: A Safe RAG-Based LLM Tutor for Programming Education](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15738)
*S M Asif Hossain,Ruksat Khan Shayoni,M. F. Mridha,Jungpil Shin*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: EduGuard是一个面向编程教育的安全RAG辅导框架，通过查询理解、课程检索、教学策略选择、评估感知生成、声明级验证和过度依赖控制等模块，在BILearn-CS基准上达到90.1%正确率、4.9%幻觉率，并将学生过度依赖从38.0%降至17.0%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在编程辅导中存在幻觉、与课程政策矛盾、泄露完整解决方案以及导致学生被动依赖等问题，亟需设计安全的生成式AI辅导框架来平衡教学支持与学习自主性。

Abstract: Generative AI (GenAI) is increasingly used by students for programming explanation, debugging, and assignment support. Yet unrestricted large language model (LLM) tutors can hallucinate, contradict course policy, reveal complete solutions, and foster passive dependence. This paper presents EduGuard, a safe retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) tutoring framework for introductory programming. EduGuard integrates query understanding, instructor-approved course retrieval, pedagogical strategy selection, rubric-aware generation, claim-level verification, and overreliance control. To make evaluation provenance explicit, we construct BILearn-CS, a 600-query instructor-authored, TA-validated benchmark spanning concept questions, debugging cases, misconceptions, assignment-support requests, code-mixed Bangla-English queries, and adversarial direct-answer prompts. Moving beyond a synthetic-only benchmark, we further evaluate on a 150-query public CS50-style course-forum set and run a small controlled pilot with 10 undergraduates using a counterbalanced pre-test/post-test design. Using Meta-Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct as the primary generator, hybrid FAISS/BM25 retrieval, and DeBERTa-v3-large-MNLI as an architecturally separate verifier, EduGuard is compared against strong baselines: GPT-4o-mini Tutor, Llama Socratic Tutor, LPITutor-style RAG, RAG with rubric prompting, and RAG with same-model self-checking. On BILearn-CS, EduGuard attains the best correctness (90.1%), grounding (89.4%), and rubric alignment (90.8%), with the lowest hallucination (4.9%) and direct-answer leakage (9.8%). In the pilot, it raises immediate post-test accuracy from 68.4% to 81.2% and cuts overreliance from 38.0% to 17.0% relative to GPT-4o-mini Tutor. These results suggest safe GenAI tutoring requires not only retrieval or strong prompting, but explicit pedagogical control, evidence verification, and deployment safeguards.

Students found feedback helpful and actionable more often than not; about a tenth thought AI unhelpful, more so towards the end of the semester. We also analyzed essay reflection depth, and used a validated AI text classifier to estimate the share of essays that could be treated as likely unaided student writing. The study contributes descriptive classroom evidence on integration of AI feedback - a fast and scalable way to provide immediate writing advice, but not a self-contained route to better reflection.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI可信度研究要么过于高层无法支持生命周期监控与再评估，要么过于狭窄的指标驱动难以对接治理需求，亟需一种既实用又可审计的方法。

Method: 提出两组件方法论：(1) 形式化框架：通过上下文敏感的协议建模治理相对可信度，使用决策树学习可解释的可信度层级规则；(2) 轻量级生命周期治理程序：包括边界余量和画像漂移两种诊断指标，以及设计时标注、部署后监控、再评估和报告的工作流。

We therefore propose a lightweight methodology for auditable trustworthiness levels in AI governance. The methodology has two components: a formal framework for representing and learning trustworthiness levels, and a lightweight AI lifecycle governance procedure for documenting, monitoring, and reassessing them over time. The formal framework models governance-relative trustworthiness through a context-sensitive protocol of measurable dimensions and learns trustworthiness levels as interpretable rules over trustworthiness profiles. Using decision trees as an interpretable proof-of-concept model class, the methodology yields explicit trustworthiness plateaus, readable level transitions, and two simple lifecycle diagnostics: boundary margins and profile drift. The governance procedure embeds these formal objects in a conformity-oriented workflow for design-time labeling, post-deployment monitoring, reassessment, and reporting. It also assigns human responsibilities and control gates for protocol design, validation, monitoring, and reassessment. We illustrate the methodology on synthetic AI lifecycle traces involving degradation, shocks, updates, heterogeneous monitoring cadences, and system comparison. Our methodology does not replace legal or other expert judgment: it supports conformity documentation and lifecycle monitoring by providing an evidential basis for documenting and tracking AI governance-relevant changes over time.

### [38] [Asymptotic fractional-order stochastic dominance with bounded relative risk aversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15317)
*Jiehua Xie,Liulei Sun,Wei Zou*

Main category: q-fin.RM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的渐近分数阶随机占优规则，用于在足够长的投资期内对投资组合进行排序。该规则基于决策者相对风险厌恶存在负下界的共识，在对数正态分布假设下建立了等价条件，并进一步提出了有界相对风险厌恶的广义渐近分数阶随机占优规则，克服了现有规则中分数阶参数对等价分布条件无影响的缺陷。实证表明新规则在长期资产选择中具有优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有渐近随机占优规则要求对数收益均值为非负，限制了其适用性；且现有渐近分数阶准则中分数阶参数对等价分布条件没有影响，缺乏灵活性。因此，需要提出一种新的规则，放宽非负约束，并使分数阶参数在等价条件中发挥作用。

Method: 基于决策者相对风险厌恶存在负下界的共识，提出渐近分数阶随机占优规则；在对数正态分布假设下推导等价条件；进一步引入边际效用条件，提出有界相对风险厌恶的广义渐近分数阶随机占优规则，并推导其分布特征等价条件。

Result: 新规则无需对数收益均值为非负的限制；广义版本使分数阶参数对等价分布条件产生实际影响；实证验证了新规则在长期资产选择中的优势。

Conclusion: 提出的渐近分数阶随机占优规则及其广义版本克服了现有规则的局限性，为长期投资决策提供了更灵活有效的排序工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a novel asymptotic fractional-order stochastic dominance rule for ranking prospects over a sufficiently long investment horizon. The new rule formulates the consensus of decision makers whose relative risk aversion has a negative lower bound. Under the assumption that returns are lognormally distributed, we establish equivalent conditions for the proposed rule without imposing the non-negativity constraint on the mean of log-return, a restriction usually required by the existing asymptotic stochastic dominance rules. Furthermore, to enhance the tractability of this asymptotic fractional-order stochastic dominance, we propose a variant of asymptotic fractional-order stochastic dominance with bounded relative risk aversion, referred to as general asymptotic fractional-order stochastic dominance, under an additional condition on decision makers' marginal utilities. We derive its corresponding equivalent distributional characterizations. The (general) asymptotic fractional-order stochastic dominance with bounded relative risk aversion overcomes the shortcomings of the existing asymptotic fractional-order criterion that the fractional-order parameter has no influence on the equivalent distributional conditions. Empirical examples further show the advantages of the newly proposed rules for asset selection in long-term investment decisions.

### [39] [On the Computational Complexity of Bilevel Integer Linear Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15369)
*Nagisa Sugishita,Margarida Carvalho*

Main category: math.OC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Jeroslow (1985) 已证明二元变量情形下双层整数线性规划是Σ^p_2-完全的，但一般整数变量的复杂度多年来悬而未决，本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 通过复杂度归约证明一般整数变量下问题仍保持Σ^p_2-完全性；同时分析结构假设对复杂度的影响，改进Köppe等人的结果，证明固定变量总数时的多项式可解性。

Result: 证明了双层整数线性规划在一般整数变量下仍是Σ^p_2-完全的；当上下层变量总数固定时，问题可在多项式时间内求解。

Conclusion: 该问题的本质难度来源于双层结构而非变量类型；固定变量总数时问题变易，为实际求解提供理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the computational complexity of bilevel integer linear programming. While Jeroslow~(1985) established that the decision version of this problem is $Σ^p_2$-complete when restricted to binary variables, we prove that this $Σ^p_2$-completeness persists even for general integer variables, settling a question that remained open for over 40 years. Furthermore, we analyze the impact of various structural assumptions on computational complexity. Notably, we strengthen the result of Köppe et al.~(2010) by proving polynomial-time solvability whenever the total number of upper- and lower-level variables is fixed, without any additional assumptions.

### [40] [Harnessing GPU Acceleration in Large-Scale Process Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15420)
*Boxun Huang,David Y. Shu,Michel Schanen,Mihai Anitescu,Rahul Gandhi,Sungho Shin*

Main category: math.OC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过程优化模型通常涉及复杂的互联单元操作、动态特性和不确定性，导致产生大规模非线性规划问题，传统CPU求解器计算负担沉重。尽管新兴的GPU求解器能提供显著计算优势，但缺乏GPU兼容的过程建模工具限制了其在过程优化中的应用。

Method: 利用现有的GPU兼容优化软件栈（ExaModels代数建模系统、MadNLP优化求解器、cuDSS线性求解器）构建原型工作流。ExaModels通过暴露重复代数结构以GPU兼容方式表述过程优化问题，MadNLP和cuDSS则在GPU上求解所得非线性规划问题。

Result: 在CO2吸收器设计问题（考虑进料不确定性）上验证，对于5000个场景、150万个变量的最大案例，GPU工作流相比使用JuMP、Ipopt和MA57的单线程CPU基线实现了约21倍的加速。

Conclusion: 该概念验证工作流成功填补了GPU求解器在过程优化中应用的空白，展示了GPU在解决大规模、含不确定性过程优化问题上的巨大潜力。

Abstract: This paper presents a proof-of-concept workflow for equation-oriented process optimization that runs entirely on a GPU. Process optimization models often incorporate complex interconnected unit operations, dynamics, and uncertainties, resulting in large nonlinear programs that can be computationally demanding for conventional CPU-based solvers. Although emerging GPU-based solvers offer substantial computational benefits, their application to process optimization has been limited by the lack of GPU-compatible process modeling tools. We address this gap by prototyping the GPU-compatible process optimization models using an existing GPU-capable optimization software stack, including ExaModels (algebraic modeling system), MadNLP (optimization solver), and cuDSS (linear solver). ExaModels formulates the process optimization problem in a GPU-compatible way by exposing its repeated algebraic structure, while MadNLP and cuDSS solve the resulting nonlinear program on the GPU. This workflow is demonstrated on a CO2 absorber design problem under feed uncertainty, in which a shared column diameter is minimized subject to equilibrium and hydraulic constraints in all scenarios. For the largest case with 5,000 scenarios and 1.5 million variables, the GPU workflow achieves a speedup of approximately 21\times over a single-threaded CPU baseline using JuMP, Ipopt, and MA57.

### [41] [A Unified Variational Framework for Optimal Transport with Lagrangian Costs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15471)
*Hailiang Liu*

Main category: math.OC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典二次代价的最优输运理论推广到一般拉格朗日代价，建立统一的变分框架来等价描述不同形式的输运距离，并揭示其背后的Hamilton结构。

Result: 得到了一个自然的最优性系统，揭示了Wasserstein空间上的Hamilton结构，建立了最优输运、Hamilton动力学和最优控制之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We investigate optimal transport distances induced by general Lagrangian action functionals. Under standard convexity assumptions on the Lagrangian, we establish the equivalence of these formulations through variational arguments and convex duality. The resulting optimality system reveals a natural Hamiltonian structure on the Wasserstein space, providing a direct link between optimal transport, Hamiltonian dynamics, and optimal control. The proposed framework extends the classical quadratic-cost theory to general Lagrangian costs and offers a unified perspective for the analysis of transport metrics generated by action functionals.

### [42] [Tropical Bi-Objective Pseudolinear Optimization as Parametric Mean-Payoff Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15481)
*Ibrahim Hassan,Abdulhadi Aminu,Lawal Muhammad*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文将参数化平均收益博弈框架扩展到双目标热带伪线性优化问题，通过双参数(λ1, λ2)平均收益博弈刻画Pareto前沿，证明了可行域和Pareto前沿的凸性及分段线性结构，给出了联合分母界等新结果，并开发了方向二分法和Newton追踪两种算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将单参数平均收益博弈框架推广到双目标热带伪线性优化场景，解决同时最小化两个热带伪线性目标的问题，并刻画其Pareto前沿的几何与组合性质。

Method: 利用双参数(λ1, λ2)平均收益博弈刻画Pareto前沿；证明可行域R和Pareto前沿P的凸性及分段线性结构；给出联合分母界定理（任意基本圈γ满足k1(γ)+k2(γ)≤2）；开发方向二分算法（伪多项式O(n²(n+m)logM)）和Newton追踪算法（通过2×2线性求解在至多|S|步内追踪完整Pareto前沿）。

Result: 可行域R为凸集，Pareto前沿P为凸分段线性曲线且仅有有限个断点；所有断点在整数数据下坐标为半整数；联合分母界|Δ|≤2（完全解耦情况除外）；方向二分算法复杂度界被随机实例验证，Newton算法的最坏情况界通过显式对抗构造证明为紧。

Conclusion: 双目标热带伪线性优化的Pareto前沿具有良好的凸分段线性几何性质，基于平均收益博弈的两种算法各有优劣：方向二分法伪多项式但可验证，Newton算法独立于数值大小但步数可能指数增长。

Abstract: We extend the parametric mean-payoff game framework of Parsons et al. to bi-objective tropical pseudolinear optimization with general two-sided constraints. The problem is to simultaneously minimize two tropical pseudolinear objectives over the feasible set of a general two-sided system U otimes x oplus b is less than or equal to V otimes x oplus d, we characterize the Pareto front via a parametric mean-payoff game in two parameters ( lambda 1, lambda 2). The feasibility region R is convex and the Pareto front P is a convex piecewise-linear curve with finitely many breakpoints, these properties are natural extensions of the single-parameter case to two parameters. In addition, we give as a new result, the joint denominator bound: the cycle coefficients satisfy k 1( gamma ) + k 2( gamma ) is less than or equal to 2 for any elementary cycle gamma, yielding | Delta | is less than or equal to 2 for every 2 times 2 Newton system, except in the fully decoupled case, and implying that all breakpoints have half-integer coordinates for integer data. Optimality and infeasibility certificates are given in terms of the cycle structure of the parametric game. Two algorithms are developed, a directional bisection algorithm (O(n squared (n+m) log M) per direction) and a Newton scheme tracing the complete Pareto front via 2 times 2 linear solves in at most | S | steps, independent of M. The directional bisection algorithm is pseudo-polynomial in n, m and M. The Newton scheme is independent of M but requires up to |S| steps, where |S| is exponential in n. Lastly, we give numerical experiments on random instances to confirm the directional bisection complexity bound exactly; the Newton scheme's worst-case bound is not attained by random instances but is shown to be tight via explicit adversarial constructions.

</details>


### [43] [Fast and Scalable Caputo Fractional Gradient Descent via Perturbation-Preserving Memory Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15505)
*Hwanseo Lee,Junseo Lee,Hyunju Kim*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出两种加速Caputo分数阶梯度下降的方法（SOE递归逼近和DHDC多尺度压缩），在保持记忆结构的同时将计算复杂度从二次降至线性或近似线性，并在强凸光滑假设下证明了压缩误差可控时的单调下降与线性收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数阶梯度下降（FGD）虽能通过Caputo算子改善病态和非凸优化问题的稳定性，但其历史依赖卷积的计算代价随迭代次数二次增长，严重限制了实际应用。本文旨在降低计算成本而不牺牲其内在记忆结构。

Method: 1) 将分数阶下降方向表达为历史梯度的离散卷积统一形式；2) 提出两种加速机制：基于指数和（SOE）逼近幂律核实现递归更新，以及新提出的二元层次离散卷积（DHDC）通过多尺度聚合策略压缩梯度历史；3) 将近似视为理想Caputo算子的扰动，分析压缩记忆对优化动力学的影响。

Result: 在μ-强凸和L-光滑假设下，当近似误差受控时，该方法仍保持单调下降和线性收敛性。

Conclusion: 通过SOE和DHDC两种互补机制，可以在保持分数阶梯度下降记忆特性的前提下显著降低计算成本，为Caputo优化方法的实际部署提供理论保证。

Abstract: Fractional gradient descent (FGD) incorporates long-range memory through Caputo-type operators and has been shown to improve stability in ill-conditioned and nonconvex optimization problems. Despite these advantages, its practical use remains limited, mainly due to the high computational cost of evaluating history-dependent convolutions, which scales quadratically with the number of iterations. In this paper, we focus on making Caputo-based optimization computationally viable without sacrificing its intrinsic memory structure. We begin by expressing the fractional descent direction as a discrete convolution over past gradients, which provides a unified view of the method. Based on this formulation, we introduce two complementary mechanisms to reduce the cost of the memory term. The first uses a sum-of-exponentials (SOE) approximation of the power-law kernel, leading to efficient recursive updates. The second approach, newly proposed in this paper as dyadic hierarchical discrete convolution (DHDC), compresses the gradient history through a multiscale aggregation strategy. Rather than treating these approximations as purely numerical accelerations, we interpret them as perturbations of the ideal Caputo operator. This viewpoint allows us to analyze how the compressed memory affects the optimization dynamics. Under standard $μ$-strong convexity and $L$-smoothness assumptions, we show that the resulting method still exhibits monotone descent and linear convergence, provided that the approximation error remains controlled.
